dfp_trap_vector(3362) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_shadow /= RIN_E_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3363) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_shadow /= R_A_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3364) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_shadow /= RIN_A_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3365) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_shadow /= V_A_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_shadow_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3366) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_shadow /= R.E.CTRL.TT( 3 DOWNTO 0 )) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3367) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_shadow /= RIN_E_CTRL_TT3DOWNTO0_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3368) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= V_D_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow_intermed_3) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3369) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3370) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= R_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3371) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= R.E.CTRL.PC( 31 DOWNTO 12 )) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3372) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= RIN_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3373) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= RIN_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3374) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= R_D_PC31DOWNTO12_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3375) <= '1' when (V_E_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= RIN_D_PC31DOWNTO12_intermed_3) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3376) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO4_shadow /= RIN_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO4_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3377) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO4_shadow /= R.A.CTRL.PC( 31 DOWNTO 4 )) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3378) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO4_shadow /= R_D_PC31DOWNTO4_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3379) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO4_shadow /= V_D_PC31DOWNTO4_shadow_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3380) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO4_shadow /= RIN_D_PC31DOWNTO4_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3381) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_shadow /= R_D_PC3DOWNTO2_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3382) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_shadow /= V_D_PC3DOWNTO2_shadow_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3383) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_shadow /= RIN_D_PC3DOWNTO2_intermed_2) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3384) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_shadow /= R.A.CTRL.PC( 3 DOWNTO 2 )) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3385) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_shadow /= RIN_A_CTRL_PC3DOWNTO2_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3386) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= V_D_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow_intermed_2) else '0';

dfp_trap_vector(3389) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= R_D_PC31DOWNTO12_intermed_1) else '0';
dfp_trap_vector(3390) <= '1' when (V_A_CTRL_PC31DOWNTO12_shadow /= RIN_D_PC31DOWNTO12_intermed_2) else '0';

dfp_or_reduce : process(dfp_trap_vector)
	variable or_reduce_1696 : std_logic_vector(1695 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_848 : std_logic_vector(847 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_424 : std_logic_vector(423 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_212 : std_logic_vector(211 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_106 : std_logic_vector(105 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_53 : std_logic_vector(52 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_27 : std_logic_vector(26 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_14 : std_logic_vector(13 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_7 : std_logic_vector(6 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_4 : std_logic_vector(3 downto 0);
	variable or_reduce_2 : std_logic_vector(1 downto 0);
begin
	or_reduce_1696 := dfp_trap_vector(3390 downto 1695) OR ("0" & dfp_trap_vector(1694 downto 0));
	or_reduce_848 := or_reduce_1696(1695 downto 848) OR or_reduce_1696(847 downto 0);
	or_reduce_424 := or_reduce_848(847 downto 424) OR or_reduce_848(423 downto 0);
	or_reduce_212 := or_reduce_424(423 downto 212) OR or_reduce_424(211 downto 0);
	or_reduce_106 := or_reduce_212(211 downto 106) OR or_reduce_212(105 downto 0);
	or_reduce_53 := or_reduce_106(105 downto 53) OR or_reduce_106(52 downto 0);
	or_reduce_27 := or_reduce_53(52 downto 26) OR ("0" & or_reduce_53(25 downto 0));
	or_reduce_14 := or_reduce_27(26 downto 13) OR ("0" & or_reduce_27(12 downto 0));
	or_reduce_7 := or_reduce_14(13 downto 7) OR or_reduce_14(6 downto 0);
	or_reduce_4 := or_reduce_7(6 downto 3) OR ("0" & or_reduce_7(2 downto 0));
	or_reduce_2 := or_reduce_4(3 downto 2) OR or_reduce_4(1 downto 0);
	or_reduce_1 <= or_reduce_2(0) OR or_reduce_2(1);
end process;

trap_enable_delay : process(clk)
begin
  if(rising_edge(clk))then
    if(rstn = '0')then
      dfp_delay_start <= 15;
    elsif(dfp_delay_start /= 0)then
      dfp_delay_start <= dfp_delay_start - 1;
    end if;
  end if;
end process;

trap_mem : process(clk)
begin
  if(rising_edge(clk))then
    if(rstn = '0')then
      dfp_trap_mem <= (others => '0');
    elsif(dfp_delay_start = 0)then
      dfp_trap_mem <= dfp_trap_mem OR dfp_trap_vector;
    end if;
  end if;
end process;

handlerTrap <= or_reduce_1 when (dfp_delay_start = 0) else '0';
